msg:Before staying at Four Seasons Tianjin, I had very low expectations, mainly because the Four Seasons in China have never been up to the standard that Four Seasons should be. We have stayed at almost all Four Seasons except those in the United States and Canada. The Four Seasons abroad are indeed absolutely top-notch, the top luxury hotel at the top of the pyramid. The Four Seasons in Guangzhou and Beijing in China are very average, and the two in Shanghai have withdrawn. Even the Four Seasons has fallen to the same level as Hilton. But I didn't expect that the Tianjin one gave me a surprise. First of all, the service. When I had breakfast, Han Yiming from Four Seasons was Ms. Elodie received us. Miss Han made us experience the long-lost service level of Four Seasons abroad. Her style of conversation, her memory and attention to our personal preferences and names, and her ability to touch the teapot with her own hands to decide whether to add hot water made us feel that Four Seasons was back. Thank you Miss Han. In addition, I like the suite room of Four Seasons Tianjin very much. I feel that it is the best hardware of Four Seasons in China. The room has golden walls, milky white doors and partitions and washbasins, rich deep yellow cabinets and window arches. The combination is very high-end and temperament, giving people a sense of spaciousness and brightness. The room is large enough, exuding a unique luxury and style of Four Seasons. I will stay there next time.

The overall style of the hotel is modern and gorgeous, and the facilities are well maintained. This time, I originally booked a premium suite, and after arriving at the hotel, I paid the difference to upgrade to the Four Seasons suite. The room is very large and magnificent. Thanks to Xiao Du at the front desk for his enthusiastic introduction and careful service. As Tianjin's top luxury brand, Four Seasons has impeccable services in all aspects, from concierge to front desk, from executive lounge to room service, which makes people feel at home. The breakfast is very rich, and the view and atmosphere of the open terrace bar in the evening are very good. The hotel gym equipment is also relatively complete, and the view of the swimming pool is excellent, but there are many children who come to learn swimming on weekends, which slightly affects the swimming experience of the guests.

We had basically stayed at Shangri-La or Ritz before, so this time we thought about trying the Four Seasons. Although the reviews were mixed, we still wanted to give the Four Seasons a chance, but we didn't expect that the impression was really bad.
First of all, due to the busy work, we didn't arrive at the hotel until 9 pm on Friday. However, Ms. Sun Qiuyang at the front desk didn't even raise her eyes when the guests came to check in, nor did she say hello. Even the handsome concierge had already put my luggage at the counter, and I had been standing in front of her for more than ten seconds without looking up at me to greet her. She kept waiting for me to open my mouth and say check in first, and then continued to say "give me your ID card" without raising her eyes. The tone was flat and the voice was low, and she didn't raise her eyes throughout the whole process. When I noted in advance that it was for my husband's birthday, she said "Happy birthday, ma'am". This attitude made us, who were already very tired, feel very uncomfortable. Although we don't pursue "respected gentlemen and ladies" like Ritz, at least basic courtesy and greetings should be achieved, right? When I came back on Saturday night, I found that she was also at work, but she was chatting and laughing with another girl behind the counter. Although there were no guests checking in, seeing the working attitude of the hotel staff did make me wonder whether I had entered the Four Seasons or an unknown one-star guesthouse.

After I got the check-in card, she continued to say without raising her eyes that the elevator was on the left hand side, but there were two elevator halls in the lobby, one for the guest room elevator and the other for the restaurant elevator. No one came out from behind the reception to guide the guests to the direct elevator to the guest room. We could only try to find it ourselves. Later, a boy at the front desk came out to guide us to the guest room elevator and expressed his apologies.

In terms of hygiene, I habitually wipe the table to check the hygiene of any room above five stars. I think it is the basic operation of the hotel to wipe the room clean and dust-free for the guests who need to stay that day, so I wiped the desk and my hands were full of dust, substantial dust.

There were birthday cards, very "small" birthday cakes and welcome fruits in the room, but the room was opposite the linen room, so the privacy was a little worse.

During the entire stay, the only person who made me feel the level of human care that the Four Seasons Hotel staff should have was Ms. Sarah Sun Xijuan who served us at breakfast. I would like to thank her and praise her very much! I only give her 1.5 points for service! Although her right hand was injured, she still insisted on working efficiently and warmly. Seeing that the meal was about to close, she helped us to serve a large plate of fruit so that we would not miss it. The next day, when we entered the restaurant, she immediately recognized us and greeted us with a very warm and enthusiastic smile. I hope that my evaluation and praise can be seen by the hotel management. The problems I encountered may also be encountered by everyone. I can only say that I hope the management will take care of themselves. If they can truly implement the problems reflected by everyone, Tianjin may be better.

No matter the service, it's not about being at home, but about making new friends. Sister Wang Jingyi, the front desk supervisor, is very kind. She showed us around the hotel, introduced Tianjin's characteristics, and helped us arrange a satisfactory room. This is very kind! Getting along with friends makes me feel the boldness of the service, rather than the "work-oriented and process-oriented" cold check-in experience. This is what I yearn for most when I stay in a hotel!
The most outstanding thing is the swimming pool. The hotel swimming pool beats everything. The landscape and changing room facilities are second to none of other hotels. In terms of sense of luxury, Four Seasons wins.
To sum it up in one sentence, come to Tianjin, live in four seasons, and the service room landscape location is like a high-level fault.
